Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204 Judicial performance survey.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(1): 78A-12-203 A third party under contract to the commission shall conduct, on an ongoing basis during the judge's term in office, the judicial performance survey required by Section
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(2): (2)(a)(i); (7)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(2)(a): The judicial performance survey shall include as respondents a sample of each of the following groups as applicable:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(2)(a)(i): attorneys who have appeared before the judge as counsel;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(2)(a)(ii): jurors who have served in a case before the judge; and
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(2)(a)(iii): court staff who have worked with the judge.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(2)(b): (2)(a)(i); (7)(a) Only a respondent under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(3): The commission may include an additional classification of respondents if the commission:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(3)(a): considers a survey of that classification of respondents helpful to voters in determining whether to vote to retain a judge; and
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(3)(b): establishes the additional classification of respondents by rule.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(4): All survey responses are confidential, including comments included with a survey response.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(5): If the commission provides information to a judge or the Judicial Council, the commission shall provide the information in such a way as to protect the anonymity of a survey respondent.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(6): A survey shall be provided to a potential survey respondent within 30 days of the day on which the case in which the person appears in the judge's court is closed, exclusive of any appeal, except for court staff and attorneys, who may be surveyed at any time during the survey period.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7): Survey categories shall include questions concerning a judge's:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(a): legal ability, including the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(a)(i): demonstration of understanding of the substantive law and any relevant rules of procedure and evidence;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(a)(ii): attentiveness to factual and legal issues before the court;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(a)(iii): adherence to precedent and ability to clearly explain departures from precedent;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(a)(iv): grasp of the practical impact on the parties of the judge's rulings, including the effect of delay and increased litigation expense;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(a)(v): ability to write clear judicial opinions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(a)(vi): ability to clearly explain the legal basis for judicial opinions;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(b): judicial temperament and integrity, including the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(b)(i): demonstration of courtesy toward attorneys, court staff, and others in the judge's court;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(b)(ii): maintenance of decorum in the courtroom;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(b)(iii): demonstration of judicial demeanor and personal attributes that promote public trust and confidence in the judicial system;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(b)(iv): preparedness for oral argument;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(b)(v): avoidance of impropriety or the appearance of impropriety;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(b)(vi): display of fairness and impartiality toward all parties; and
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(b)(vii): ability to clearly communicate, including the ability to explain the basis for written rulings, court procedures, and decisions; and
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(c): administrative performance, including the following:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(c)(i): management of workload;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(c)(ii): sharing proportionally the workload within the court or district; and
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(7)(c)(iii): issuance of opinions and orders without unnecessary delay.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(8): If the commission determines that a certain survey question or category of questions is not appropriate for a respondent group, the commission may omit that question or category of questions from the survey provided to that respondent group.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(9): 
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(9)(a): The survey shall allow respondents to indicate responses in a manner determined by the commission, which shall be:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(9)(a)(i): on a numerical scale from one to five; or
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(9)(a)(ii): in the affirmative or negative, with an option to indicate the respondent's inability to respond in the affirmative or negative.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(9)(b): 
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-204(9)(b)(i): To supplement the responses to questions on either a numerical scale or in the affirmative or negative, the commission may allow respondents to provide written comments.

Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207 Evaluation of justice court judges.
--------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(1): The Judicial Performance Evaluation Commission shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(1)(a): conduct a performance evaluation for each justice court judge in the third and fifth year of the justice court judge's term;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(1)(b): classify each justice court judge into one of the following three categories:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(1)(b)(i): full evaluation;
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(1)(b)(ii): midlevel evaluation; or
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(1)(b)(iii): basic evaluation; and
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(1)(c): establish evaluation criteria for each of the three categories.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(2): A full evaluation justice court judge shall be subject to the requirements of this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(3): 78A-12-204 A midlevel evaluation justice court judge shall be governed by this chapter, except as provided below:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(3)(a): 78A-12-204 the commission shall administer an intercept survey periodically outside the courtroom of the evaluated justice court judge in lieu of the survey specified in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(3)(b): courtroom observation may not be conducted for midlevel evaluation justice court judges.
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(4): A basic evaluation justice court judge shall be governed by this chapter, except as provided below:
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(4)(a): basic evaluation justice court judges shall comply with minimum performance standards for judicial education, judicial conduct, cases under advisement, and any other standards the commission may promulgate by administrative rule; and
Utah Code Annotated § 78A-12-207(4)(b): courtroom observation and surveys may not be conducted for basic evaluation justice court judges.
